| 2:20:14| which was established in 1996 as the Knoxville Hate Crimes Working Group.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110516special?start=8414)|

| 2:20:29| law enforcement agencies, and concerned citizens who work together to help defeat and prevent hate crimes,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110516special?start=8429)|
